content[match.start() :]\n   101→    preamble_bytes = len(preamble.encode(\"utf-8\"))\n   102→\n   103→    # Atomic write: tmp file + os.replace\n   104→    tmp_file = output_file.with_suffix(output_file.suffix + \".tmp\")\n   105→    tmp_file.write_text(cleaned, encoding=\"utf-8\")\n   106→    os.replace(tmp_file, output_file)\n   107→\n   108→    _log.info(\"Stripped %d-byte preamble from %s\", preamble_bytes, output_file)\n   109→    return preamble_bytes\n   110→\n   111→\n   112→def _inject_pipeline_diagnostics(\n   113→    output_file: Path,\n   114→    started_at: datetime,\n   115→    finished_at: datetime,\n   116→) -> None:\n   117→    \"\"\"Inject executor-populated pipeline_diagnostics into extraction frontmatter.\n   118→\n   119→    The LLM cannot reliably produce execution timing or environment metadata,\n   120→    so the executor injects these fields post-subprocess (FR-033).\n   121→    \"\"\"\n   122→    content = output_file.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n   123→    if not content.startswith(\"---\"):\n   124→        return\n   125→\n   126→    # Find end of frontmatter\n   127→    end_idx = content.find(\"\\n---\", 3)\n   128→    if end_idx == -1:\n   129→        return\n   130→\n   131→    elapsed = (finished_at - started_at).total_seconds()\n   132→    diagnostics_line = (\n   133→        f\"pipeline_diagnostics: \"\n   134→        f\"{{elapsed_seconds: {elapsed:.1f}, \"\n   135→        f\"started_at: \\\"{started_at.isoformat()}\\\", \"\n   136→        f\"finished_at: \\\"{finished_at.isoformat()}\\\"}}\"\n   137→    )\n   138→\n   139→    # Insert before the closing ---\n   140→    new_content = (\n   141→        content[: end_idx]\n   142→        + \"\\n\"\n   143→        + diagnostics_line\n   144→        + content[end_idx:]\n   145→    )\n   146→    output_file.write_text(new_content, encoding=\"utf-8\")\n   147→\n   148→\n   149→def roadmap_run_step(\n   150→    step: Step,\n   151→    config: PipelineConfig,\n   152→    cancel_check: Callable[[], bool],\n   153→) -> StepResult:\n   154→    \"\"\"Execute a single roadmap step as a Claude subprocess.\n   155→\n   156→    Builds argv with context isolation, launches process, waits with\n   157→    timeout, and returns StepResult.\n   158→    \"\"\"\n   159→    started_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n   160→\n   161→    if config.dry_run:\n   162→        _log.info(\"[dry-run] Would execute step '%s'\", step.id)\n   163→        return StepResult(\n   164→            step=step,\n   165→            status=StepStatus.PASS,\n   166→            attempt=1,\n   167→            started_at=started_at,\n   168→            finished_at=datetime.now(timezone.utc),\n   169→        )\n   170→\n   171→    # Inline embedding: read input files into the prompt instead of --file flags\n   172→    embedded = _embed_inputs(step.inputs)\n   173→    if embedded and len(embedded.encode(\"utf-8\")) <= _EMBED_SIZE_LIMIT:\n   174→        effective_prompt = step.prompt + \"\\n\\n\" + embedded\n   175→        extra_args: list[str] = []\n   176→    elif embedded:\n   177→        _log.warning(\n   178→            \"Step '%s': embedded inputs exceed %d bytes, falling back to --file flags\",\n   179→            step.id,\n   180→            _EMBED_SIZE_LIMIT,\n   181→        )\n   182→        effective_prompt = step.prompt\n   183→        extra_args = [\n   184→            arg\n   185→            for input_path in step.inputs\n   186→            for arg in (\"--file\", str(input_path))\n   187→        ]\n   188→    else:\n   189→        effective_prompt = step.prompt\n   190→        extra_args = []\n   191→\n   192→    proc = ClaudeProcess(\n   193→        prompt=effective_prompt,\n   194→        output_file=step.output_file,\n   195→        error_file=step.output_file.with_suffix(\".err\"),\n   196→        max_turns=config.max_turns,\n   197→        model=step.model or config.model,\n   198→        permission_flag=config.permission_flag,\n   199→        timeout_seconds=step.timeout_seconds,\n   200→        output_format=\"text\",\n   201→        extra_args=extra_args,\n   202→    )\n   203→\n   204→    proc.start()\n   205→\n   206→    # Poll for cancellation while waiting\n   207→    while proc._process is not None and proc._process.poll() is None:\n   208→        if cancel_check():\n   209→            proc.terminate()\n   210→            return StepResult(\n   211→                step=step,\n   212→                status=StepStatus.CANCELLED,\n   213→                attempt=1,\n   214→                gate_failure_reason=\"Cancelled by external signal\",\n   215→                started_at=started_at,\n   216→                finished_at=datetime.now(timezone.utc),\n   217→            )\n   218→        time.sleep(1)\n   219→\n   220→    exit_code = proc.wait()\n   221→    finished_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n   222→\n   223→    if exit_code == 124:\n   224→        return StepResult(\n   225→            step=step,\n   226→            status=StepStatus.TIMEOUT,\n   227→            attempt=1,\n   228→            gate_failure_reason=f\"Step '{step.id}' timed out after {step.timeout_seconds}s\",\n   229→            started_at=started_at,\n   230→            finished_at=finished_at,\n   231→        )\n   232→\n   233→    if exit_code != 0:\n   234→        return StepResult(\n   235→            step=step,\n   236→            status=StepStatus.FAIL,\n   237→            attempt=1,\n   238→            gate_failure_reason=f\"Step '{step.id}' exited with code {exit_code}\",\n   239→            started_at=started_at,\n   240→            finished_at=finished_at,\n   241→        )\n   242→\n   243→    # Sanitize output: strip conversational preamble before gate validation\n   244→    _sanitize_output(step.output_file)\n   245→\n   246→    # Inject executor-populated fields into extract step frontmatter (FR-033)\n   247→    if step.id == \"extract\" and step.output_file.exists():\n   248→        _inject_pipeline_diagnostics(step.output_file, started_at, finished_at)\n   249→\n   250→    # Process completed successfully; gate check happens in execute_pipeline\n   251→    return StepResult(\n   252→        step=step,\n   253→        status=StepStatus.PASS,\n   254→        attempt=1,\n   255→        started_at=started_at,\n   256→        finished_at=finished_at,\n   257→    )\n   258→\n   259→\n   260→def _build_steps(config: RoadmapConfig) -> list[Step | list[Step]]:\n   261→    \"\"\"Build the 9-step pipeline with parallel generate group.\n   262→\n   263→    Returns a list where 394→\n   395→def _format_halt_output(results: list[StepResult], config: RoadmapConfig) -> str:\n   396→    \"\"\"Format HALT diagnostic output per spec section 6.2.\"\"\"\n   397→    failed = [r for r StepStatus.CANCELLED]\n   400→\n   401→    if not failed:\n   402→        return \"\"\n   403→\n   404→    fail = failed[-1]\n   405→    step = fail.step\n   406→\n   407→    # Calculate file details len(content.encode(\"utf-8\"))\n   412→        line_count = len(content.splitlines())\n   413→        file_info = f\"  Output size: {byte_count} bytes ({line_count} lines)\\n\"\n   414→    elif step:\n   415→        file_info = \"  Output file: not created\\n\"\n   416→\n   417→    elapsed = f\"{fail.duration_seconds:.0f}s\"\n   418→\n   419→    lines = [\n   420→        f\"ERROR: Roadmap pipeline halted at step '{step.id}' (attempt {fail.attempt}/2)\",\n   421→        f\"  Gate failure: {fail.gate_failure_reason}\",\n   422→        f\"  Output file: {step.output_file}\",\n   423→ attempt {r.attempt})' for r in passed) or 'none'}\",\n   427→        f\"Failed step:     {step.id} ({fail.status.value}, attempt {fail.attempt})\",\n   428→    ]\n   429→\n   430→    # Collect skipped steps\n   431→    all_step_ids = _get_all_step_ids(config)\n   432→    executed_ids = {r.step.id for r in results}\n   433→    skipped_ids = [sid for sid in all_step_ids if sid not in executed_ids]\n 521→\n   522→\n   523→def _save_state(config: RoadmapConfig, results: list[StepResult]) -> None:\n   524→    \"\"\"Write .roadmap-state.json to output_dir via atomic tmp + os.replace().\n   525→\n \"\"\"Derive fidelity_status enum from a spec-fidelity StepResult.\n   574→\n   575→    Returns one of: 'pass', 'fail', 'skipped', 'degraded'.\n   576→    \"\"\"\n   577→    if result.status == 584→    if result.status == StepStatus.SKIPPED:\n   585→        return \"skipped\"\n   586→    if result.status in (StepStatus.FAIL, StepStatus.TIMEOUT):\n   587→        return \"fail\"\n   588→ \"\"\"Generate a degraded fidelity report when the agent fails.\n   597→\n   598→    Produces a report with validation_complete=false and\n   599→    fidelity_check_attempted=true so the \"---\\n\"\n   614→        \"\\n\"\n   615→        \"## Degraded Fidelity Report\\n\"\n   616→        \"\\n\"\n   617→        \"Spec-fidelity validation could not be completed.\\n\"\n   618→ 634→\n   635→\n   636→def write_state(state: dict, path: Path) -> None:\n   637→    \"\"\"Write state dict to path atomically via tmp file + os.replace().\"\"\"\n   638→    import os as _os\n   639→\n   640→    path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n   641→    tmp = path.with_suffix(\".tmp\")\n   642→    tmp.write_text(json.dumps(state, indent=2), encoding=\"utf-8\")\n   643→  648→    if not path.exists():\n   649→        return None\n   650→    try:\n   651→        text = path.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n   652→        if not text.strip():\n   653→            return \"\"\"Strip conversational preamble before YAML frontmatter in a step output file.\n\n    Reads the file, finds the first ``^---`` line, and removes everything before\n    it.  Uses atomic write (write to ``.tmp`` then ``os.replace()``) to prevent\n    partial file states.\n\n    Returns the byte count of the stripped preamble (0 when file already starts\n    with ``---`` or 0\n\n    # Already starts with frontmatter delimiter -- nothing to strip\n    if content.lstrip().startswith(\"---\"):\n        return 0\n\n    # Search for the first ^--- line\n    match = re.search(r\"^---[ \\t]*$\", content, re.MULTILINE)\n    if match is None:\n        # No frontmatter found at all -- leave file unchanged\n        return 0\n\n    preamble = content[: match.start()]\n    cleaned = content[match.start() :]\n    preamble_bytes = len(preamble.encode(\"utf-8\"))\n\n    # Atomic write: tmp file + os.replace\n    tmp_file = output_file.with_suffix(output_file.suffix + preamble_bytes\n\n\ndef _inject_pipeline_diagnostics(\n    output_file: Path,\n    started_at: datetime,\n    finished_at: datetime,\n) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Inject executor-populated pipeline_diagnostics into extraction frontmatter.\n\n    The LLM cannot reliably produce execution timing or environment metadata,\n    so the executor injects these fields post-subprocess (FR-033).\n    \"\"\"\n    content = output_file.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n    if not content.startswith(\"---\"):\n        return\n\n    # Find end of frontmatter\n    end_idx = content.find(\"\\n---\", roadmap_run_step(\n    step: Step,\n    config: PipelineConfig,\n    cancel_check: Callable[[], bool],\n) -> StepResult:\n    \"\"\"Execute a single roadmap step as a Claude subprocess.\n\n    Builds argv with context isolation, launches process, waits with\n    timeout, and returns StepResult.\n    \"\"\"\n    started_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n\n    if config.dry_run:\n        _log.info(\"[dry-run] Would execute step '%s'\", step.id)\n        return StepResult(\n            step=step,\n            status=StepStatus.PASS,\n            attempt=1,\n            started_at=started_at,\n            finished_at=datetime.now(timezone.utc),\n        )\n\n    # Inline embedding: read input files into the prompt instead of --file flags\n    embedded = _embed_inputs(step.inputs)\n    if embedded and len(embedded.encode(\"utf-8\")) <= _EMBED_SIZE_LIMIT:\n        effective_prompt = step.prompt + \"\\n\\n\" + embedded\n        extra_args: list[str] = []\n    elif embedded:\n        _log.warning(\n            \"Step '%s': embedded inputs exceed %d bytes, falling back to --file flags\",\n            step.id,\n            _EMBED_SIZE_LIMIT,\n        )\n        effective_prompt = step.prompt\n        extra_args = [\n            arg\n            for input_path in step.inputs\n            for arg in (\"--file\", str(input_path))\n        ]\n    else:\n        effective_prompt = step.prompt\n        extra_args = []\n\n    proc = ClaudeProcess(\n        prompt=effective_prompt,\n        output_file=step.output_file,\n        error_file=step.output_file.with_suffix(\".err\"),\n        max_turns=config.max_turns,\n        model=step.model or config.model,\n        permission_flag=config.permission_flag,\n        timeout_seconds=step.timeout_seconds,\n        output_format=\"text\",\n        extra_args=extra_args,\n    )\n\n    proc.start()\n\n    # Poll for cancellation while waiting\n    while proc._process is not None and proc._process.poll() is None:\n        if cancel_check():\n            proc.terminate()\n            return StepResult(\n                step=step,\n                status=StepStatus.CANCELLED,\n                attempt=1,\n                gate_failure_reason=\"Cancelled by external signal\",\n                started_at=started_at,\n                finished_at=datetime.now(timezone.utc),\n            )\n        time.sleep(1)\n\n    exit_code = proc.wait()\n    finished_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n\n    if exit_code == 124:\n        return StepResult(\n            step=step,\n            status=StepStatus.TIMEOUT,\n            attempt=1,\n            gate_failure_reason=f\"Step '{step.id}' timed out after {step.timeout_seconds}s\",\n            started_at=started_at,\n            finished_at=finished_at,\n        )\n\n    if exit_code != 0:\n        return StepResult(\n            step=step,\n            status=StepStatus.FAIL,\n            attempt=1,\n            gate_failure_reason=f\"Step '{step.id}' exited with code {exit_code}\",\n            started_at=started_at,\n            finished_at=finished_at,\n        )\n\n    # Sanitize output: strip conversational preamble before gate validation\n    _sanitize_output(step.output_file)\n\n    # Inject executor-populated fields into extract step frontmatter (FR-033)\n    if step.id == \"extract\" and step.output_file.exists():\n        _inject_pipeline_diagnostics(step.output_file, started_at, finished_at)\n\n    # Process completed successfully; gate check happens in execute_pipeline\n    return StepResult(\n        step=step,\n        status=StepStatus.PASS,\n        attempt=1,\n        started_at=started_at,\n        finished_at=finished_at,\n    )\n\n\ndef _build_steps(config: RoadmapConfig) -> list[Step | list[Step]]:\n    \"\"\"Build the 9-step pipeline with parallel generate group.\n\n    Returns a list where each element is either a single Step (sequential)\n    or a list[Step] (parallel group).\n    \"\"\"\n    out = config.output_dir\n\n    # Agent specs\n    agent_a = config.agents[0]\n    agent_b = config.agents[1] if len(config.agents) > 1 else config.agents[0]\n\n    # Output paths\n    extraction = out / \"extraction.md\"\n    roadmap_a = out / f\"roadmap-{agent_a.id}.md\"\n    roadmap_b = out / f\"roadmap-{agent_b.id}.md\"\n    diff_file = out / \"diff-analysis.md\"\n    debate_file = out / \"debate-transcript.md\"\n    score_file = out / \"base-selection.md\"\n    merge_file = out / \"roadmap.md\"\n    test_strat = out / \"test-strategy.md\"\n    spec_fidelity_file = out / \"spec-fidelity.md\"\n\n    # Load retrospective content if configured (missing file handled gracefully)\n    retrospective_content: str | None = None\n    if config.retrospective_file is not None and config.retrospective_file.is_file():\n        try:\n            retrospective_content = config.retrospective_file.read_text(\n                encoding=\"utf-8\"\n            )\n        except OSError:\n            retrospective_content = None\n\n    steps: list[Step | list[Step]] = [\n        # Step 1: Extract\n        Step(\n            id=\"extract\",\n            prompt=build_extract_prompt(\n                config.spec_file,\n                retrospective_content=retrospective_content,\n            ),\n Generate (parallel)\n        [\n            Step(\n                id=f\"generate-{agent_a.id}\",\n                prompt=build_generate_prompt(agent_a, extraction),\n                output_file=roadmap_a,\n                gate=GENERATE_A_GATE,\n                timeout_seconds=900,\n                inputs=[extraction],\n                retry_limit=1,\n                model=agent_a.model,\n            ),\n            Step(\n                id=f\"generate-{agent_b.id}\",\n                prompt=build_generate_prompt(agent_b, extraction),\n                output_file=roadmap_b,\n                gate=GENERATE_B_GATE,\n                timeout_seconds=900,\n                inputs=[extraction],\n                retry_limit=1,\n                model=agent_b.model,\n            ),\n        ],\n        # Step 3: Diff\n        Step(\n            id=\"diff\",\n            prompt=build_diff_prompt(roadmap_a, roadmap_b),\n            output_file=diff_file,\n            gate=DIFF_GATE,\n            timeout_seconds=300,\n            inputs=[roadmap_a, roadmap_b],\n            retry_limit=1,\n        ),\n        # Step 4: Debate\n        Step(\n            id=\"debate\",\n            prompt=build_debate_prompt(diff_file, roadmap_a, roadmap_b, config.depth),\n            output_file=debate_file,\n            gate=DEBATE_GATE,\n            timeout_seconds=600,\n            inputs=[diff_file, roadmap_a, roadmap_b],\n            retry_limit=1,\n        ),\n        # Step 5: Score\n        Step(\n            id=\"score\",\n            prompt=build_score_prompt(debate_file, roadmap_a, roadmap_b),\n            output_file=score_file,\n            gate=SCORE_GATE,\n            timeout_seconds=300,\n            inputs=[debate_file, roadmap_a, roadmap_b],\n            retry_limit=1,\n        ),\n        # Step 6: Merge\n        Step(\n            id=\"merge\",\n            prompt=build_merge_prompt(score_file, roadmap_a, roadmap_b, debate_file),\n            output_file=merge_file,\n            gate=MERGE_GATE,\n            timeout_seconds=600,\n            inputs=[score_file, roadmap_a, roadmap_b, debate_file],\n            retry_limit=1,\n        ),\n        # Step 7: Test Strategy\n        Step(\n            id=\"test-strategy\",\n            prompt=build_test_strategy_prompt(merge_file, extraction),\n            output_file=test_strat,\n            gate=TEST_STRATEGY_GATE,\n            timeout_seconds=300,\n            inputs=[merge_file, extraction],\n            retry_limit=1,\n        ),\n        # Step 8: Spec Fidelity (after test-strategy, FR-008 through FR-010)\n        Step(\n            id=\"spec-fidelity\",\n            prompt=build_spec_fidelity_prompt(config.spec_file, merge_file),\n            output_file=spec_fidelity_file,\n            gate=SPEC_FIDELITY_GATE,\n            timeout_seconds=600,\n            inputs=[config.spec_file, merge_file],\n            retry_limit=1,\n        ),\n    ]\n\n    return steps\n\n\ndef _format_halt_output(results: list[StepResult], config: RoadmapConfig) -> str:\n    \"\"\"Format HALT diagnostic output per spec section 6.2.\"\"\"\n    failed = [r for r in results if r.status in (StepStatus.FAIL, StepStatus.TIMEOUT)]\n    passed = [r for r in results if r.status == StepStatus.PASS]\n    cancelled = [r for r in results if r.status == StepStatus.CANCELLED]\n\n    if not failed:\n        return \"\"\n\n    fail = failed[-1]\n    step = fail.step\n\n    # Calculate file details if output exists\n    file_info = \"\"\n    if step and {fail.attempt})\",\n    ]\n\n    # Collect skipped steps\n    all_step_ids = _get_all_step_ids(config)\n    executed_ids = {r.step.id for r in results}\n    skipped_ids = [sid for sid in all_step_ids \"spec-fidelity\",\n    ]\n\n\ndef _print_step_start(step: Step) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Print progress output when a step starts.\"\"\"\n    print(f\"[roadmap] Starting step: {step.id}\", 'fail', 'skipped', 'degraded'.\n    \"\"\"\n    if result.status == StepStatus.PASS:\n        # Check if the output indicates degraded mode\n        if result.step and \"fail\"\n    return \"skipped\"\n\n\ndef generate_degraded_report(\n    output_file: Path,\n    failed_agent: str,\n    failure_reason: str,\n) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Generate a degraded fidelity report dict, path: Path) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Write state dict to path atomically via tmp file + os.replace().\"\"\"\n    import os as _os\n\n    path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n    tmp = Preserves milestone-internal ordering: deliverables within each\n    milestone maintain their relative order after decomposition.\n    \"\"\"\n    return decompose_deliverables(deliverables)\n\n\ndef execute_roadmap(config: RoadmapConfig, resume: bool = False, no_validate: bool = False) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Execute the roadmap generation pipeline.\n\n    Builds the step list, handles --dry-run and --resume, then\n    delegates to execute_pipeline() with roadmap_run_step.\n\n    After all 9 steps pass, auto-invokes validation unless\n    --no-validate is set or --resume halted on a failed step.\n\n    Note: --no-validate does NOT skip the spec-fidelity step\n    (FR-010, AC-005). It only skips the post-pipeline validation\n    subsystem.\n    \"\"\"\n    config.output_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n\n    steps = _build_steps(config)\n\n    # --dry-run: print plan and exit\n    if config.dry_run:\n        _dry_run_output(steps)\n        return\n\n    # --resume: check which steps already pass their gates\n    if resume:\n        from ..pipeline.gates import gate_passed\n\n        steps = _apply_resume(steps, config, gate_passed)\n\n    # Execute pipeline\n    results = execute_pipeline(\n        steps=steps,\n        config=config,\n        run_step=roadmap_run_step,\n        on_step_start=_print_step_start,\n        on_step_complete=_print_step_complete,\n    )\n\n    # Save state\n    _save_state(config, results)\n\n    # Check for failures\n    failures = [r for r in results if r.status in (StepStatus.FAIL, StepStatus.TIMEOUT)]\n    if failures:\n        halt_msg = _format_halt_output(results, config)\n        print(halt_msg, file=sys.stderr)\n        sys.exit(1)\n\n    print(f\"\\n[roadmap] Pipeline complete: {len(results)} steps passed\", flush=True)\n\n    # Auto-invoke validation after successful pipeline completion\n    if no_validate:\n        print(\"[roadmap] Validation skipped (--no-validate)\", flush=True)\n        _save_validation_status(config, \"skipped\")\n        return\n\n    # Check if validation already completed (--resume path)\n    if resume:\n        state_file = config.output_dir / \".roadmap-state.json\"\n        state = read_state(state_file)\n        if state and \"validation\" in state:\n            saved = state[\"validation\"]\n            if saved.get(\"status\") in (\"pass\", \"fail\"):\n                print(\n                    f\"[roadmap] Validation already completed ({saved['status']}), skipping\",\n                    flush=True,\n                )\n                return\n\n    _auto_invoke_validate(config)\n\n\ndef _save_validation_status(\n    config: RoadmapConfig,\n    status: str,\n) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Update .roadmap-state.json with validation status.\n\n    Adds or updates the ``validation`` key without modifying existing state.\n\n    Parameters\n    ----------\n    config:\n        RoadmapConfig with output_dir.\n    status:\n        One of \"pass\", \"fail\", or \"skipped\".\n    \"\"\"\n    state_file = config.output_dir / \".roadmap-state.json\"\n    state = read_state(state_file)\n    if state is None:\n        state = {}\n    state[\"validation\"] = {\n        \"status\": status,\n        \"timestamp\": roadmap pipeline run.\n\n    Inherits --model, --max-turns, --debug from the parent roadmap config.\n    Default agent count for roadmap-run invocation is 2 (dual-agent for rigor).\n    \"\"\"\n    from .models import AgentSpec, ValidateConfig\n    from .validate_executor import execute_validate\n\n    # Default to 2 agents for roadmap-run auto-invocation (dual-agent for rigor per OQ-1)\n    validate_agents = config.agents[:2] if len(config.agents) >= 2 else config.agents\n\n    validate_config = ValidateConfig(\n        output_dir=config.output_dir,\n        agents=validate_agents,\n        work_dir=config.output_dir,\n        max_turns=config.max_turns,\n        model=config.model,\n        debug=config.debug,\n    )\n\n    print(\"\\n[roadmap] Auto-invoking validation...\", flush=True)\n\n    try:\n        counts = execute_validate(validate_config)\n        blocking = counts.get(\"blocking_count\", 0)\n        warning = counts.get(\"warning_count\", 0)\n        info = counts.get(\"info_count\", 0)\n        print(\n            f\"[validate] Complete: {blocking} blocking, {warning} warning, {info} info\",\n            flush=True,\n        )\n        validation_status = \"fail\" if blocking > 0 else \"pass\"\n        _save_validation_status(config, validation_status)\n    except FileNotFoundError as exc:\n        _log.error(\"Validation skipped: %s\", exc)\n        print(f\"[validate] Skipped: {exc}\", file=sys.stderr, flush=True)\n        _save_validation_status(config, \"skipped\")\n\n\ndef _apply_resume(\n    steps: list[Step | list[Step]],\n    config: RoadmapConfig,\n    gate_fn: Callable,\n) -> list[Step | list[Step]]:\n    \"\"\"Apply --resume logic: skip steps whose outputs already pass gates.\n\n    Also checks for stale spec detection.\n    \"\"\"\n    state_file = config.output_dir / \".roadmap-state.json\"\n    state = read_state(state_file)\n    force_extract = False\n    if state is not None:\n        saved_hash = state.get(\"spec_hash\", \"\")\n        current_hash = hashlib.sha256(config.spec_file.read_bytes()).hexdigest()\n        if saved_hash and saved_hash != current_hash:\n            print(\n                f\"WARNING: spec-file has changed since last run.\\n\"\n                f\"  Last hash: {saved_hash[:12]}...\\n\"\n                f\"  Current:   {current_hash[:12]}...\\n\"\n                f\"Forcing re-run of extract step.\",\n                file=sys.stderr,\n                flush=True,\n            )\n            force_extract = True\n\n    skipped = 0\n    result: list[Step | list[Step]] = []\n    found_failure = False\n\n    for entry in steps:\n        if found_failure:\n            # After first failing step, include all remaining steps\n            result.append(entry)\n            continue\n\n        if isinstance(entry, list):\n            # Parallel group: check all steps\n            all_pass = True\n            for s in entry:\n                if s.gate:\n                    passed, _reason = gate_fn(s.output_file, s.gate)\n                    if not passed:\n                        all_pass = False\n                        break\n                else:\n                    all_pass = False\n                    break\n            if all_pass:\n                skipped += len(entry)\n                print(f\"[roadmap] Skipping {', '.join(s.id for s in entry)} (gates pass)\", flush=True)\n            else:\n                found_failure = True\n                result.append(entry)\n        else:\n            # Force re-run of extract on stale spec\n            if force_extract and entry.id == \"extract\":\n                found_failure = True\n                result.append(entry)\n                continue\n\n            if entry.gate:\n                passed, _reason = gate_fn(entry.output_file, entry.gate)\n                if passed:\n                    skipped += 1\n                    print(f\"[roadmap] Skipping Atomic write: tmp file + os.replace\n    tmp_file = output_file.with_suffix(output_file.suffix + \".tmp\")\n    tmp_file.write_text(cleaned, encoding=\"utf-8\")\n    os.replace(tmp_file, output_file)\n\n    _log.info(\"Stripped %d-byte preamble from %s\", preamble_bytes, output_file)\n    return preamble_bytes\n\n\ndef _inject_pipeline_diagnostics(\n    output_file: Path,\n    started_at: datetime,\n    finished_at: datetime,\n) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Inject executor-populated pipeline_diagnostics into extraction frontmatter.\n\n    The LLM cannot reliably produce execution timing or environment metadata,\n    so the executor injects these fields post-subprocess (FR-033).\n    \"\"\"\n    content = output_file.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n    if not content.startswith(\"---\"):\n        return\n\n    # Insert before the closing ---\n    new_content = (\n        content[: end_idx]\n        + \"\\n\"\n        + diagnostics_line\n        + content[end_idx:]\n    )\n    output_file.write_text(new_content, encoding=\"utf-8\")\n\n\ndef roadmap_run_step(\n    step: Step,\n    config: PipelineConfig,\n    cancel_check: Callable[[], bool],\n) -> StepResult:\n    \"\"\"Execute a single roadmap step as a Claude subprocess.\n\n    Builds argv with context isolation, launches process, waits with\n    timeout, and returns StepResult.\n    \"\"\"\n    started_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n\n    if config.dry_run:\n        _log.info(\"[dry-run] Would execute step '%s'\", step.id)\n        return StepResult(\n            step=step,\n            status=StepStatus.PASS,\n            attempt=1,\n            started_at=started_at,\n            finished_at=datetime.now(timezone.utc),\n        )\n\n    # Inline embedding: read input files into the prompt instead of --file flags\n    embedded = _embed_inputs(step.inputs)\n    if embedded and len(embedded.encode(\"utf-8\")) <= _EMBED_SIZE_LIMIT:\n        effective_prompt = step.prompt + \"\\n\\n\" + embedded\n        extra_args: list[str] = []\n    elif embedded:\n        _log.warning(\n            \"Step '%s': embedded inputs exceed %d bytes, falling back to --file flags\",\n            step.id,\n            _EMBED_SIZE_LIMIT,\n        )\n        effective_prompt = step.prompt\n        extra_args = [\n            arg\n            for input_path in step.inputs\n            for arg in (\"--file\", str(input_path))\n        ]\n    else:\n        effective_prompt = step.prompt\n        extra_args = []\n\n    proc = ClaudeProcess(\n        prompt=effective_prompt,\n        output_file=step.output_file,\n        error_file=step.output_file.with_suffix(\".err\"),\n        max_turns=config.max_turns,\n        model=step.model or config.model,\n        permission_flag=config.permission_flag,\n        timeout_seconds=step.timeout_seconds,\n        output_format=\"text\",\n        extra_args=extra_args,\n    )\n\n    proc.start()\n\n    # Poll for cancellation while waiting\n    while proc._process is not None and proc._process.poll() is None:\n        if cancel_check():\n            proc.terminate()\n            return StepResult(\n                step=step,\n                status=StepStatus.CANCELLED,\n                attempt=1,\n                gate_failure_reason=\"Cancelled by external signal\",\n                started_at=started_at,\n                finished_at=datetime.now(timezone.utc),\n            )\n        time.sleep(1)\n\n    exit_code = proc.wait()\n    finished_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n\n    if exit_code == 124:\n        return StepResult(\n            step=step,\n            status=StepStatus.TIMEOUT,\n            attempt=1,\n            gate_failure_reason=f\"Step '{step.id}' timed out after {step.timeout_seconds}s\",\n            started_at=started_at,\n            finished_at=finished_at,\n        )\n\n    if exit_code != 0:\n        return StepResult(\n            step=step,\n            status=StepStatus.FAIL,\n            attempt=1,\n            gate_failure_reason=f\"Step '{step.id}' exited with code {exit_code}\",\n            started_at=started_at,\n            finished_at=finished_at,\n        )\n\n    # Sanitize output: strip conversational preamble before gate validation\n    _sanitize_output(step.output_file)\n\n    # Inject executor-populated fields into extract step frontmatter (FR-033)\n    if step.id == \"extract\" and step.output_file.exists():\n        _inject_pipeline_diagnostics(step.output_file, started_at, finished_at)\n\n    # Process completed successfully; gate check happens in execute_pipeline\n    return StepResult(\n        step=step,\n        status=StepStatus.PASS,\n        attempt=1,\n        started_at=started_at,\n        finished_at=finished_at,\n    )\n\n\ndef build_certify_step(\n    config: RoadmapConfig,\n    findings: list | None = None,\n    context_sections: dict[str, str] | None = None,\n) -> Step:\n    \"\"\"Build a certify Step for execution via execute_pipeline().\n\n    The certify step runs as a standard Step (not ClaudeProcess directly)\n    per spec section 2.5. \"\"\"Format HALT diagnostic output per spec section 6.2.\"\"\"\n    failed = [r for r in results if r.status in (StepStatus.FAIL, StepStatus.TIMEOUT)]\n    passed = [r for r in results if r.status == execute_roadmap(config: RoadmapConfig, resume: bool = False, no_validate: bool = False) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Execute the roadmap generation pipeline.\n\n    Builds the step list, handles --dry-run and --resume, then\n    delegates to execute_pipeline() with roadmap_run_step.\n\n    After all 9 steps pass, auto-invokes validation unless\n    --no-validate is set or --resume halted on a failed It only skips the post-pipeline validation\n    subsystem.\n    \"\"\"\n    config.output_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n\n    steps = _build_steps(config)\n\n    # --dry-run: print plan and exit\n    if config.dry_run:\n        _dry_run_output(steps)\n        return\n\n    # --resume: check which steps already pass their gates\n    if resume:\n        from ..pipeline.gates import gate_passed\n\n        steps = _apply_resume(steps, config, gate_passed)\n\n    # Execute pipeline\n    results = execute_pipeline(\n        steps=steps,\n        config=config,\n        run_step=roadmap_run_step,\n        on_step_start=_print_step_start,\n        on_step_complete=_print_step_complete,\n    )\n\n    # Save state\n    _save_state(config, results)\n\n    # Check for failures\n    failures = [r for r in results if r.status in (StepStatus.FAIL, StepStatus.TIMEOUT)]\n    if failures:\n        halt_msg = _format_halt_output(results, config)\n        print(halt_msg, print(f\"[validate] Skipped: {exc}\", file=sys.stderr, flush=True)\n        _save_validation_status(config, \"skipped\")\n\n\ndef _apply_resume(\n    steps: list[Step | list[Step]],\n    config: RoadmapConfig,\n    gate_fn: Callable,\n) -> list[Step | list[Step]]:\n    \"\"\"Apply --resume logic: skip steps whose outputs already pass gates.\n\n    Also checks for stale spec detection.\n    \"\"\"\n    state_file = config.output_dir / \".roadmap-state.json\"\n    state = read_state(state_file)\n    force_extract = False\n    if state is not None:\n        saved_hash = state.get(\"spec_hash\", \"\")\n        current_hash = hashlib.sha256(config.spec_file.read_bytes()).hexdigest()\n        if saved_hash and saved_hash != current_hash:\n            print(\n                f\"WARNING: spec-file has changed since last run.\\n\"\n                f\"  Last hash: {saved_hash[:12]}...\\n\"\n                f\"  Current:   {current_hash[:12]}...\\n\"\n                f\"Forcing re-run of extract step.\",\n                file=sys.stderr,\n                flush=True,\n            )\n            force_extract = True\n\n    skipped = 0\n    result: list[Step | list[Step]] = []\n    found_failure = False\n\n    for entry in steps:\n        if found_failure:\n            # After first failing step, include all remaining steps\n            result.append(entry)\n            continue\n\n        if isinstance(entry, list):\n            # Parallel group: check all steps\n            all_pass = True\n            for s in entry:\n                if s.gate:\n                    passed, _reason = gate_fn(s.output_file, s.gate)\n                    if not passed:\n                        all_pass = False\n                        break\n                else:\n                    all_pass = False\n                    break\n            if all_pass:\n                skipped += len(entry)\n                print(f\"[roadmap] Skipping {', '.join(s.id for s in entry)} (gates pass)\", flush=True)\n            else:\n                found_failure = True\n                result.append(entry)\n        else:\n            # Force re-run of extract on stale spec\n            if force_extract and entry.id == \"extract\":\n                found_failure = True\n                result.append(entry)\n                continue\n\n            if entry.gate:\n                passed, _reason = gate_fn(entry.output_file, entry.gate)\n                if passed:\n                    skipped += 1\n                    print(f\"[roadmap] Skipping {entry.id} (gate passes)\", flush=True)\n                    continue\n            found_failure = True\n            result.append(entry)\n\n    if skipped > 0:\n        print(f\"[roadmap] Skipped {skipped} steps (gates pass)\", flush=True)\n\n    if not result:\n        print(\"[roadmap] All steps already pass gates.
